Issue #9147: Labels: type/enhancement
Issue #9146: Labels: No Labels
I have analyzed the root cause of the issue and its solutions.\n\nRoot Cause of the Issue\n\nThe issue arises because the default value of pullBatchSize in the Go Pull Consumer is set to 0. In RocketMQ‚Äôs implementation, maxMsgNums (which corresponds to pullBatchSize) cannot be 0, as this prevents correct access to the logical queue.\n\nSpecifically:\n\t1.\tIn your code, you did not set consumer.WithPullBatchSize(), which caused the default value of 0 to be used.\n\t2.\tWhen this value is sent to the server, stricter parameter checks in the RocksDB storage mode result in message pull failures.\n\t3.\tIn the default ConsumeQueue storage mode, this issue might not be apparent due to fault tolerance mechanisms, but in RocksDB mode, it directly fails.\n\nSolutions\n\nShort-term Solution:\nExplicitly set pullBatchSize when creating the Pull Consumer:\n\npullConsumer, err = rocketmq.NewPullConsumer(\n    consumer.WithGroupName(consumerGroupName),\n    consumer.WithNameServer(nameSrv),\n    consumer.WithMaxReconsumeTimes(2),\n    consumer.WithPullBatchSize(32), // Add this line and set a reasonable value (1-1024)\n)\n\nLong-term Solutions:\n\t1.\tSet a reasonable default value (e.g., 32) for pullBatchSize in the Go client.\n\t2.\tAdd parameter validation to ensure that pullBatchSize falls within a valid range (1-1024).\n\t3.\tImprove the documentation to clearly explain the requirements and limitations of this parameter.

Issue #9084: Labels: No Labels
Issue #9083: Labels: No Labels
This is a protection measure. When a broker scales out, the registered topic route might become visible to Producers first, causing some messages to be sent. If the Consumer starts consuming from the latest offset at this time, these messages would be skipped.

When sending a message, if the producer status is not RUNNING, this error will be reported. You should check if the producer failed to execute start or for other reasons.

This pull request does fix something that is broken. However, this is a design error to replicate bits here and there from one node to the other.  \r\n\r\nWAL should the the ONLY data structure that is replicated among nodes and it contains source of truth for everything, including offset advancement of each consumer that is managed in the sever side.
